```python
from selenium import webdriver
```


```python
url = "https://wuhanvirus.kr/"

driver = webdriver.Chrome('c:/informs/chromedriver.exe')

driver.implicitly_wait(3)
driver.get(url)
```


```python
# 지역 '전체' 클릭하기 
driver.find_element_by_id('전체').click()
```


```python
# 정렬 클릭하기
driver.find_element_by_id('patient-reorder').click()
```


```python
html = driver.page_source
type(html)
```




    str




```python
# print(html)
```


```python
# driver.close()
```


```python

```


```python
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
import pandas as pd
```


```python
soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'html.parser')
```


```python
type(soup)
```




    bs4.BeautifulSoup




```python
# print(soup)
```


```python
sum1 = soup.select('tr.summary.first > td')

sum1_result = []

for td in sum1:
    sum1_txt = td.text
    sum1_result.append(sum1_txt)
    print(sum1_txt)
    if sum1_txt == '#U17':
        break
```

```python
def chunker(seq, size):
    return (seq[pos:pos + size] for pos in range(0, len(seq), size))
```


```python
sum1_results = []

for group1 in chunker(sum1_result, 5):
    group1 = group1
    sum1_results.append(group1)
    print(group1)
```

```python
sum2 = soup.select('tr.summary.second > td')

sum2_result = []

    sum2_txt = td.text
    sum2_result.append(sum2_txt)
    print(sum2_txt)
```

```python
sum2_results = []

for group2 in chunker(sum2_result, 5):
    group2 = group2
    sum2_results.append(group2)
    print(group2)
```
